 kya hai ye 'G' kaa jhamela?2g, 3G or 4G main aane vaale 'G' se matlab mobile takneekee kii jenereshan se he
 Just as the new generation is considered faster than the older generation, 4G is also faster than its older generation technologies (3G, 2G, 1G)
 internet seva main pehali donon peedi 1G or 2G kaa naata analog se he vanhi 3G or 4G digital duniya kii takneekee he
 So what does 4G mean? 4G is the fourth generation of wireless service
 3G takanic main OFDMA (orthogonal frequency divijan multiple acces) kii sahaayta se network kii suvidha ko or behatar banaaya jaataa he
 4G will be a fully IP based service
 isamen wais, data or multimedia ko samaan gati se bheja or risive kiya ja sakegaa
 How much better than 3G? To say, 3G has all the facilities that have the potential to change a lot in the world of technology
 par 4G kaa koi jawaab nahin
 The speed of 4G is 100 to 300 Mbps which is 50 times more than 3G
 3G ke mukaable 4G kaa data rate zyada he yani data kaa transfar tej gati se kiya ja saktaa he
 Also, the price of this technology is also expected to be lower than 3G, because with the arrival of 4G, consumption is also being projected to increase more than double
 3G takanic jahaan wide aria network par kaam karti he, vanhi 4G local aria network (LAN) or base stesan wide aria network par kaam karti he
 4G Vs
 3G ?speed:3g : adhiktam 3
 1 Mbps and 1 on average 300 Kbps
 5 mbps4g : amuman 2-40 Mbps par 100 se 300 Mbps tak badhaaye jane kii kshamta

 Want to face inflation or recession? Choose your problem
 philhal to donon hi badhane vaali hai
 According to the Reserve Bank, inflation will increase in the next three months
 or is saal kii duusari timahi main vikaas dar 4
 5 percent is not the end of this slope
 agle chah maah main mandi gahraaegi
 This year the growth rate of five percent is also impossible
 bachat, khapat or nivesh main kami se bani yah mandi jitani uljhan bhari he, mahangaai usase kam pechida nahin he
 It is understandable only after the peeling of inflation that the Reserve Bank has stopped the reduction in interest rates, and has moved the government to fight the recession and on the other hand the government is unable to understand which inflation is good
 And what is the worst or how to break this pair of recession and inflation? ‚Ä¢ Wholesale inflation in the month of October at the lowest level of 40 months (0
 16 fisad) thi, jabaki khudara mahangaai 16 maheene ke sarvocch str 4
 At 6 percent
 thok mahangaai utpaadakon ke str par keemton kii napjokh he jabaki khudara mahangaai upabhoktaaon kii jeb par asar kii paimaaish karti he
 The record decrease in wholesale inflation is evidence of demand breakdown due to which producers (farmers and industry) are not able to raise prices
 is saal rabi mausam tak krishi or khaadya utpaadon kii keemten laagat se kam thim
 The prices of manufacturing products have not increased for the past several months
 duusari taraf, khudara yani upabhokta mahangaai is saal janvari se badhane lagi thi jo ab sarkaar ko daraane vaale str tak aa gai
 Wholesale inflation is evidence of slowdown in consumption and retail inflation is expensive consumption
 donon kaa ek saath prakat hona maang or aapurti donon main dhanchaagat dikkaton kaa durlabh duryog he‚Ä¢ mahangaai kaa doosraa pech yah he ki aapurti kii dikkaton ke kaaran falon-subjiyon vaali khaadya mahangaai bad rahi he jabaki maang main kami ke kaaran gharelu khapat ke saamaan, sevaaon, bhawan nirmaan, sanchaar keemton main badhotaree nahin hui he yani utpaadakon ke laabh nahin bad rahe hai
 ‚Ä¢ Another major challenge is the difference between urban and rural inflation
 aktubar ke maheene main gaanvon main khaadya mahangaai badhane kii dar 6
 4 percent while 10 in cities
 5 fisad
 ‚Ä¢ Another face of inflation measurement increases the confusion manifold
 care retings ke ek taaja adhyayan ke anusaar, pichley vitt varsh main bharat ke 19 rajyon main upabhokta mahangaai, rashtriya ausat se zyada rahi jabaki 11 rajyon main rigerv bank ke adarsh paimaane (4 fisad) se upar thi, yani ki hamaare pados kii mahangaai, desh kii mahangaai se bilkul alag he
 In light of the recession, the contradiction of inflation has put the economy in a state of difficult choices
 puraa utpaadan kshetra mandi kaa shikaar he
 This includes both farmers and industry
 2014 se 2019 ke bich kheti main kamai badhane kii raftaar isse pehle ke dashak kii tulana main aadhi rahi thi
 It is important to increase prices from both the farmer and industry point of view because now the wheel of consumption cannot revolve without increasing income and employment
 achraj nahin ki mandi ke baavjood mobile bill or kuch kaaron kii keemat main ijapha shuru ho gaya he

 khaastaur par rojgaar dene vaale udyogon main mandi ke kaaran nai naukariyaan band hai or vetan main badhat bhi

 mahangaai yaa keemton main badhotaree bharat main samvedansheel paimaana he

 Unnecessary intervention of governments has spoiled the market
 haal ke varshon main bharat main nunatam mahangaai ke baad bhi maang nahin badi
 Now the imbalance of policies is stifling

 Renowned Hindi litterateur Namvar Singh has died at the age of 92
 ve pichley ek maheene se dilli ke ames aspataal ke troma centre main bhartee the
 Namvar Singh was called the creator of criticism in Hindi literature
 unke lekhan par jitani charchaa hui, utani hi charchaa unke kathanon or bhaashanon par bhi kii gai thi
 He is credited with giving new heights to criticism and interview mode
 kavita ke nae pratimaan ke liye 1971 main namvar singh ko sahitya academy puraskaar se nawaja gaya tha
 Namwar Singh was born on 28 July 1927 in Jeyanpur (now Chandauli) Varanasi
 unhone kaashi hindu vishvavidhyalay se hindi sahitya main eme or piechdi kii or uske baad unhone kai varshon tak vahaan padhaayaa bhi
 Along with BHU, he taught at Sagar, Jodhpur University, Agra University
 phir wo dilli ke jeenyu main aa gaye or vahiin se ritair hue
 Namwar Singh was also very knowledgeable in Urdu
 ve 'aalochana' tremasik ke pradhan sampadak rahe or unhone 'janyug' saptahik (1965-67) kaa sampadan bhi kiya
 Raja Rammohan Roy was the president of the library establishment since 1992
 adhyaapan or lekhan ke alaava unhone raajnneeti main bhi haath aajamaaya tha
 He got into active politics in the year 1959 and this year he contested Lok Sabha election from chakia-chandauli seat under the Communist Party of India banner
 haalanki is chunaav main unhen haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa tha

 saakshaatkaar:kahana na hogasampadit granth:kahani: nai kahani, kavita ke naye pratimaan, duusari parampara kii khoj, vaad vivaad samvaad, kahana na hoga
 Chintamani Part-3, Ramchandra Shukla Sanchayan, Hazariprasad Dwivedi: Compiled Essays, Today's Hindi Story, Modern Teaching Russian Poems, Forerunners of the Renaissance: Balakrishna Bhatt
